***wel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> (39)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wela</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wala</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wela</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*welh₁-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wohl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">well</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href = vnd.unilang:vel.html>vel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">väl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no"><a href = vnd.unilang:vel.html>vel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>The opposite of not (used to add positive emphasis to the verb, much like the auxiliaries "do" or "does" in affirmative sentences in English)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dacht.html>dacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> golf <a href = vnd.unilang:hield.html>hield</a>?  |  <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hou.html>hou</a> <b>wél</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> golf!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I thought you didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> like golf?  |  I <b>do</b> like golf!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziet.html>ziet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>...</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You [can] <b>certainly</b> see that...</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>ken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>do</b> know him, but not well.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>Maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Well then, what <i><b>do</b></i> you want?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>no less than, as much as, as many as <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">expressing amazement</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:twaalf.html>twaalf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewerkt.html>gewerkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> worked <b>no less than</b> twelve <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a> today!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fairly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voel.html>voel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardig.html>aardig</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I feel <b>fairly</b> decent, but not really good.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> well
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> does, that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>well</b> done.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">"<a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedacht.html>gedacht</a>," <a href = vnd.unilang:zeide.html>zeide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">"That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>well</b> thought through, " he <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>In sense 1, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often strongly stressed (especially when directly contradicting a negative statement or question) and therefore written with an <a href = vnd.unilang:accent.html>accent</a>: <i>wél</i>.</li>
<li>Using <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> as adverbial form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a>. Usually, the adjective <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in its bare form (as with other adjectives).</li>
<li>The use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> in the sense of "fairly", while quite idiomatic, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very unemphatic. When translating to English, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> to leave it out.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the adverb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">weal</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">general state of <span class="Latn" lang="en">well-being</span> and prosperity</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wellen.html>welle</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wella</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wallijō</i>.
</p>

</p>

***welbespraakt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:welbespraakt.html>welbespraakt</a> (22354)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bespreken.html>bespraakt</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welbespraakt.html>welbespraakt</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welbespraakt.html>welbespraakter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">welbespraaktst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">well-spoken</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">eloquent</span></li></ol>

<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wiljakumô</i>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welks.html>welks</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> whose
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wee.html>Wee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:welks.html>welks</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:koning.html>koning</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></i>
<dl><dd>Woe to the country <b>whose</b> king <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a child</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

For masculine <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> in the singular, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used; <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> for feminine <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> in the singular and for all plurals.

***welletjes.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:welletjes.html>welletjes</a> (14875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-etje</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welletjes.html>welletjes</a></strong> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">invariable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> enough
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:welletjes.html>welletjes</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That’s quite <b>enough</b> already!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:welletjes.html>Welletjes</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only used predicatively and usually expresses mild annoyance, but also <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an ironic connotation, as if one <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> talking to a child.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***wellicht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wellicht.html>wellicht</a> (2137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">villicht</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">villîcht</i> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">villicht</i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">vielleicht</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wellicht.html>wellicht</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sentence-initial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> possibly, perhaps
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wellicht.html>Wellicht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trein.html>trein</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemist.html>gemist</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Perhaps</b> he missed the train.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>probably, likely
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wellicht.html>wellicht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:helpen.html>helpen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This will <b>probably</b> help.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Used as the opening word of a sentence, the term tends to indicate a lower degree of confidence.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:welp.html>welp</a> (28395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:welp.html>welp</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:welp.html>welp</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwelpaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welp.html>welp</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welpen.html>welpen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welpje.html>welpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>whelp, young mammal of certain carnivorous species, notably canine pup, bear <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> or lion cub</li>
<li>human youngster, especially of age group 8-11 in boy <a href = vnd.unilang:scouts.html>scouts</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:welvaartsstaat.html>welvaartsstaat</a> (96947)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welvaart.html>welvaart</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">welfare state</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welvaartsstaat.html>welvaartsstaat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welvaartsstaat.html>welvaartsstaten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welvaartsstaat.html>welvaartsstaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">welfare state</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwannē</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wending.html>wending</a> (14773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wenden.html>wenden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wending.html>wending</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wendingen.html>wendingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wending.html>wendingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">wendinkje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***wenkbrauw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wenkbrauw.html>wenkbrauw</a> (24324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wintbrauwe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wintbrāwa</i>. The first element <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unknown but presumed to be related to Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἴονθος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">íonthos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The second element <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brēwō</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wimper.html>wimper</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eyelash</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from a contraction.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wenkbrauw.html>wenkbrauw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wenkbrauwen.html>wenkbrauwen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wenkbrauw.html>wenkbrauwtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eyebrow</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">brauw</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wenkbrauw.html>wenkbrauw</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:anatomie.html>anatomie</a>)</span> knokige <a href = vnd.unilang:rand.html>rand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oog.html>oog</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:meestal.html>meestal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begroeid.html>begroeid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a>

***wenken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wenken.html>wenken</a> (32146)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wenken.html>wenken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wenken.html>wenken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wankijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wenken.html>wenken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to beckon, wave</li>
<li>to warn by hinting with body movements</li></ol>

***wens.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wens.html>wens</a> (1184)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wensch</i>, next to eastern <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wonsch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wunsk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wunskaz</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wunsch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wish</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">winsk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">ønske</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wentelen.html>wentelen</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>

</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To rotate, turn <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To revolve, wind</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To wallow, roll <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></li></ol>

***wentelteefje.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wentelteefje.html>wentelteefje</a> (110870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<span id="rfv-etymology-notice-nl-"></span>Can this<sup class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Etymology_scriptorium/2020/Augustamp;action=editamp;section=newamp;preload=Template:rfv-etymology/preloadamp;preloadtitle=%5B%5Bwentelteefje%23rfv-etymology-notice-nl-%7cwentelteefje%5D%5D">+</a>)</sup> etymology be sourced?)</span>
For the first part, compare the older ‘ghewendt broot’ (variants: ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:gewonden.html>gewonden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a>’, ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:gewonnen.html>gewonnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a>’) which meant ‘bread soaked in eggs, confectionery bread’. The meaning could be related to soaking, to turning around (of either the egg mixture or the bread) or <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> to winning something back (they're traditionally made from stale bread; compare French ‘pain perdu’).
</p><p>The origin of the second part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> completely unknown, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> variously theorised to have got something to do with baking, confectionery, or a slice of bread. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> possible (but not known) that the form of this part changed under influence of the word ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:teef.html>teef</a>’.
</p><p>There are also various folk etymologies, like ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:wentel.html>wentel</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a>’ (just flip it) or ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:wentel.html>wentel</a>’ (flip) + ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:teef.html>teef</a>’ (<a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a>), but these are unlikely when the older <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> are <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> into consideration. The interpretation of the second part as ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a>’ <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> influence the Frisian word for French <a href = vnd.unilang:toast.html>toast</a>: ‘brette hânsfuotsjes’.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wentelteefje.html>wentelteefje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wentelteefjes.html>wentelteefjes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>French <a href = vnd.unilang:toast.html>toast</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gewonnen.html>gewonnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a></span></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Belgium</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">sometimes used as a pet name for women;</span> Cutie Pie, <a href = vnd.unilang:cupcake.html>Cupcake</a>, Candy, Pumpkin</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more common to use the plural form; the singular form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only used when referring to one specific piece.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wentelteefje.html>wentelteefje</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>  <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:boterham.html>boterham</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geweekt.html>geweekt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:melk.html>melk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eieren.html>eieren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarna.html>daarna</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebakken.html>gebakken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meestal.html>meestal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontbijt.html>ontbijt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eet.html>eet</a>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:troetelnaam.html>troetelnaampje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwen.html>vrouwen</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nationale.html>nationale</a> vrouwenspotgids, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boekje.html>boekje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarin.html>waarin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> 76 vrouwtypes <a href = vnd.unilang:onderscheidt.html>onderscheidt</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wentelteefje.html>wentelteefje</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> kibbelvrouwtje, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> zeurscheur). <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***wereld.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a> (283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">werelt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">werold</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">werolt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weraldiz</i>, from Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weraz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aldiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time, age, old</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, hence "age of <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>".
</p><p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wrâld</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">world</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:welt.html>Welt</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">värld</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werelden.html>werelden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wereldje.html>wereldje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>world</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The genitive form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">'s <a href = vnd.unilang:werelds.html>werelds</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still in common use.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></li>

<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> Romeinse <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wereldrijk.html>wereldrijk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> ongeëvenaarde <a href = vnd.unilang:nalatenschap.html>nalatenschap</a>, in <a href = vnd.unilang:tegenstelling.html>tegenstelling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> Parthische <a href = vnd.unilang:rivaal.html>rivaal</a></i>

***werk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> (180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">werc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*werką</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wérǵom</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werkje.html>werkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>task, job, chore
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebeuren.html>gebeuren</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voltooid.html>voltooid</a>.</i>  |  The thing that must be done <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> finished.</dd></dl></li>
<li>profession (line of work)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buschauffeur.html>buschauffeur</a>.</i>  |  The profession of <a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a> driver.</dd></dl></li>
<li>workplace
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a>.</i>  |  Today <a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> arrived to the workplace too late.</dd></dl></li>
<li>product (result of work)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Magritte <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veiling.html>veiling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkocht.html>verkocht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a>.</i>  |  The work of Magritte will be <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> by auction.</dd></dl></li>

***werkeloos.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:werkeloos.html>werkeloos</a> (15220)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werkeloos.html>werkeloos</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>having nothing to do, doing nothing; idle, workless
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:werkeloos.html>werkeloos</a></b> toezien</i> — to watch <b>idly</b> (doing nothing to help)</dd></dl></li>
<li>workless, jobless, unemployed
<ul><li><b>1770</b> August 6, “Groot <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Brittanien”, <i>Leydse Maandagſche <a href = vnd.unilang:courant.html>Courant</a></i> No. 94, page 1:
<dl><dd>Veele Scheeps <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Timmerlieden , <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:werkeloos.html>werkeloos</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> , zyn <a href = vnd.unilang:bereid.html>bereids</a> in dienſt genoomen , ...
<dl><dd>Many ship <a href = vnd.unilang:carpenters.html>carpenters</a> who <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> unemployed have already <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> into service, ...</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In recent years, some writers have started to make a distinction between the alternative forms <i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkloos.html>werkloos</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkeloos.html>werkeloos</a></i>, reserving the former for the sense “unemployed” and the latter for the sense “idle”. This distinction <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> no historical basis.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:werkeloos.html>werkeloos</a></b> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> (344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wirken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wirkijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to work, make</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*werǵ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to work, act</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work, labour</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work, to be effective</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to function, be in working order</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> amateur radio</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to contact</li></ol>

***werker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:werker.html>werker</a> (9014)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werker.html>werker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werkers.html>werkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werker.html>werkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werkster.html>werkster</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>worker</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
